"In his book Our America: Nativism, Modernism and Pluralism (1995), Walter Benn Michaels argues that modernism and nativism emerged together in American literature in the 1920s through their mutual commitment to resolve the meaning of identity _ linguistic, national, cultural and racial (2-3).     Thus nativism depends on understanding oneês Americanness as racial difference as evidenced in texts by modernist writers as diverse as Willa Cather, William Faulkner and William Carlos Williams.",
